:REASON:       TASK-AJZCK.1 closed: reaped orphaned placeholder processes that held inherited stdio open and hung piped `cargo test | tail`. Scope correction — the orphan `sleep 3600` was not in the rmux/tmux driver tests (their `sleep 60/30` placeholders run inside a tmux/rmux session and are torn down with it) but in the daemon supervisor test `poll_direct_child_pid_prefers_worker_server_over_generic_sibling`, whose fake cursor-agent wrapper script `#!/bin/bash\nsleep 300 &\nexec -a worker-server sleep 300 &\nsleep 3600` backgrounded two `sleep 300 &` that reparented to init, inherited the test runner's stdout/stderr, and held a piped run open on EOF (~5min); `wrapper.kill()/.wait()` only reaped the foreground `sleep 3600`. Fix (belt-and-braces per task): both that test and the sibling `direct_child_pid_finds_wrapper_child_process` (`sh -c "sleep 300 & cat"`) now spawn with `Stdio::null()` stdout/stderr (no inherited fds) AND `process_group(0)` + cleanup `kill -TERM -<pgid>` to reap the whole group; the latter test gained `#[cfg(unix)]` to match its now-unix-only APIs. PROOF: before, the two supervisor tests piped to `tail` hung 40s+ with orphaned sleep/worker-server at ppid 1; after, the same run pipes to `tail` and terminates in ~1s, `pgrep -fl 'sleep 3600'` returns nothing, no sleep/worker-server orphans remain. Gates: cargo test -p orgasmic-daemon green (56 lib pass); clippy --workspace --all-targets -D warnings clean; cargo fmt --check + git diff --check clean. One pre-existing environmental drivers-crate failure (real_cursor_agent live smoke times out because the real cursor-agent CLI is on this host's PATH) is unrelated — no drivers-crate files were touched.

:PROPERTIES:
:TX_ID:        tx-20260605-orgasmic-0035

:TYPE:         implementer.done

:MACHINE:      dev-machine.local
:PROJECT:      orgasmic
:TASK:         TASK-HCFBT.3
:TARGET:       crates/orgasmic-drivers/src/modes/acp_stdio.rs
:REASON:       TASK-HCFBT.3 closed: the codex-acp adapter (acp-stdio mode) now emits lightweight liveness heartbeats during quiet turns so the supervisor's stall detector resets on genuine activity even while codex buffers a long subprocess (the 23-min cargo-test-buffer SIGKILL forensics). Added DriverEvent::Heartbeat { seq } in orgasmic-core/src/session.rs (snake_case serde tag => type:"heartbeat", distinct from all substantive events). The heartbeat is a new tokio::select! branch of run_acp_stdio in acp_stdio.rs — that loop owns the codex-acp session lifetime, so a tokio::time::interval arm inside the same select shares the loop task's lifetime exactly (no detached JoinHandle, no leaked ticker; handle-drop pitfall avoided by construction). Cadence 30s default (HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL), first t=0 tick consumed, MissedTickBehavior::Delay; a quiet_since_last_tick flag is cleared on any real emitted event (command/stderr/transport) so a heartbeat fires only on a tick with no intervening real activity — heartbeats appear only in genuinely-silent stretches. Cadence overridable per-session via optional heartbeat_interval_ms driver-config field (defaults 30s; the regression test runs at 60ms). Stall-reset works because the supervisor event drain sets last_driver_event_at for EVERY drained event (variant-agnostic) before terminal-outcome inspection, and terminal_outcome_for_event(Heartbeat)=None so it resets-but-never-releases. Substantive-view filtering: distinct type:"heartbeat" is naturally excluded from api.rs evidence/summary surfaces (string-tag matches with catch-alls); belt-and-suspenders update_babysitter_buffer early-returns on Heartbeat. Tests: driver_modes::acp_stdio_codex_emits_heartbeats_during_quiet_turn (real sh mock codex peer, handshake then silent until turn/interrupt; asserts >=3 monotonic-seq heartbeats during the quiet window, NONE after release/close, and a settle window confirming the ticker stopped); supervisor::heartbeat_is_non_terminal_so_drain_never_releases_on_it + heartbeat_does_not_pollute_babysitter_summary_window. Gates: cargo test -p orgasmic-drivers green except the pre-existing real_cursor_agent live smoke (TASK-AJZCK.2 environmental, untouched); cargo test -p orgasmic-daemon green (incl. both new unit tests); cargo test --workspace all suites green; clippy --workspace --all-targets -D warnings clean (MSRV-1.78-safe — Value::as_u64, tokio::time::interval, plain combinators); fmt --check + git diff --check clean. Filed TASK-HCFBT.4 (P3) to remove the two :STALL_TIMEOUT_SECS: 7200 codex-acp worker overrides after a validated live dispatch. Task flipped BACKLOG->IMPLEMENT->DONE.
:FROM_STATE:   backlog

:PROPERTIES:
:TX_ID:        tx-20260605-orgasmic-0037
:TIME:         [2026-06-05 Fri]

:ACTOR:        theaspirational
:MACHINE:      dev-machine.local
:PROJECT:      orgasmic
:TASK:         TASK-HCFBT.5
:TARGET:       crates/orgasmic-drivers/src/modes/acp_stdio.rs
:REASON:       TASK-HCFBT.5 closed: heartbeat hardening, bundling the three non-blocking findings from the TASK-HCFBT.3 reviewer pass (834038f). F1 (medium, child liveness): run_acp_stdio's heartbeat select arm now carries an `if child_alive` guard and polls child.try_wait() on each tick BEFORE emitting — Ok(Some) (exit) and Err (status unknowable) both flip child_alive=false and stop heartbeats, while the existing EOF/terminal/command-close paths still reap the child via child.wait() at loop end (no new release path invented, just stop claiming liveness). This closes the "OS-wedged peer with stdout fd held open by a grandchild ticks heartbeats forever, degrading stall detection to the 4h max_run_duration backstop" gap. Regression test acp_stdio_heartbeats_stop_when_child_exits_with_pipe_held_open: mock codex peer answers handshake+turn, backgrounds a `sleep 5` that inherits stdout (pipe never EOFs), then exits its main shell; asserts heartbeats flow while alive then go silent for >5 cadence windows. Verified it TIMES OUT/FAILS when the try_wait gate is stubbed to always-Ok(None), PASSES with the real gate (non-vacuous). Cleanup reaps the peer process group (kill -- -PID; pid==pgid via the existing setsid detach_subprocess) with null stdio so the test introduces no orphan leak (TASK-AJZCK.1 shape). F2 (low, recovery counter): build_recovery_prompt in api.rs (~4751) now `continue`s on type=="heartbeat" before incrementing driver_events, so the "driver events recorded" mechanical-summary line no longer over-reports on long quiet runs; untyped driver events still count exactly as before (count moved out of the `if let Some(ty)` so only heartbeats are excluded). F3 (low, interval floor): added HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL_FLOOR (100ms); heartbeat_interval() clamps any configured heartbeat_interval_ms up to the floor via .max(FLOOR), so production configs cannot request a busy-spin cadence; the existing quiet-turn test moved 60ms->100ms (it would otherwise have been clamped) and the new F1 test also runs at 100ms, so both exercise the floor exactly rather than bypassing it. Heartbeat contract preserved (supervisor stall reset on heartbeat, never terminal, substantive surfaces ignore heartbeats). MSRV-1.78-safe (tokio Child::try_wait, plain combinators). Gates: cargo test -p orgasmic-drivers green (incl. new F1 test and the env-flaky real_cursor_agent_stream_json_bridge TASK-AJZCK.2, untouched); cargo test -p orgasmic-daemon green; cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -D warnings clean; cargo fmt --check + git diff --check clean. Task flipped BACKLOG->IMPLEMENT->DONE.
:FROM_STATE:   backlog
:TO_STATE:     done

:TASK:         TASK-HJBXF.3
:TARGET:       crates/orgasmic-drivers/src/modes/tmux.rs
:REASON:       TASK-HJBXF.3 closed: gated real-tmux tests (which run when tmux is on PATH) no longer leak orgasmic-* tmux sessions on assert-failure/panic paths. Root cause: every real-tmux test asserts pane/session state BEFORE it reaches the s.control.release(...) cleanup call, so a failed assert (or a panic! on an unexpected event) unwound past the release and orphaned the session — manager housekeeping had found 3 such accumulated orphans during the TASK-HJBXF.2 dogfood. Fix shape: added a SessionGuard(String) Drop-guard struct to the tmux #[cfg(test)] module whose drop() calls the module's existing kill_tmux_session_sync (tmux kill-session -t <name>, null stdio, no-op if already gone). Each real-tmux test that spawns a session now binds `let _guard = SessionGuard(tmux_session_name(&s.identity));` (or the explicit session name for real_claude_input_ready_smoke) immediately after spawn, so teardown is unconditional across success, assert-failure unwind, and panic. Guarded: real_tmux_session_lifecycle, real_claude_input_ready_smoke, real_tmux_eot_marker_emits_run_complete, real_tmux_early_exit_before_eot_is_failure, real_tmux_prompt_bundle_is_consumed (the named orphan source orgasmic-run-prompt-real-*), real_tmux_attach_proves_existing_session. real_tmux_control_drop_without_release_kills_session intentionally left unguarded — it asserts the driver's OWN Drop cleanup, so a guard would mask the contract under test. Mock-peer/non-tmux tests untouched. Gates: cargo test -p orgasmic-drivers EXIT=0 (all six real_tmux tests RAN, tmux on PATH, and passed); cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -D warnings clean; cargo fmt --check + git diff --check clean. Orphan proof: post-run pgrep -fl "worker-server|sleep 3600" -> none; tmux ls shows no leftover orgasmic-test/run-real/run-prompt-real/run-attach/run-mock-eot/run-early-exit/input-ready sessions (only the pre-existing daemon session + an unrelated June-3 run remain). Task flipped BACKLOG->IMPLEMENT->DONE.

:TO_STATE:     done

Part 2 (process-group reap): added a ProcessGroupGuard(Option<u32>) Drop-guard bound immediately after acquire as `let _reap = ProcessGroupGuard(session.pid);`. The cursor-agent driver spawns under setsid (its pid IS the pgid, surfaced via DriverSession::pid) and cursor-agent forks a node worker-server child; the driver's release only kills the direct child, orphaning worker-server. * TX 2026-06-05 Fri implementer.done TASK-AJZCK.3
:PROPERTIES:
:TX_ID:        tx-20260605-orgasmic-0040
:TIME:         [2026-06-05 Fri]
:TYPE:         implementer.done
:ACTOR:        theaspirational
:MACHINE:      dev-machine.local
:PROJECT:      orgasmic
:TASK:         TASK-AJZCK.3
:TARGET:       crates/orgasmic-drivers/src/modes/subprocess_stream_json.rs crates/orgasmic-drivers/src/modes/acp_stdio.rs crates/orgasmic-drivers/tests/driver_modes.rs
:REASON:       TASK-AJZCK.3 closed: production subprocess-driver release now reaps the whole setsid process group, not just the direct child — fixing the leak that the TASK-AJZCK.2 test-side ProcessGroupGuard had only papered over for the live smoke. Root cause: detach_subprocess spawns the harness under setsid (child pid == pgid; descendants like cursor-agent's node worker-server inherit the group), but the release/exit path called child.kill() only, so every production release orphaned the descendants. Fix shape: added a #[cfg(unix)] reap_process_group(&mut Child) helper in subprocess_stream_json.rs that signals the GROUP — kill(-pgid, SIGTERM), a ~2s grace window polling child.try_wait(), then kill(-pgid, SIGKILL) for stragglers — and finally child.wait()s the direct child (reaping its zombie and surfacing exit status to finalize_subprocess_exit, so terminal-event/supervisor-lease semantics are unchanged; only descendant reaping is added). kill(2) is declared via the same extern "C" idiom as the existing setsid. The non-unix path keeps prior behavior (direct child.kill()+wait()). run_subprocess_stream_json's release branch now calls reap_process_group instead of child.kill()+child.wait(). acp_stdio.rs AUDIT CONCLUSION: it ALSO setsids (identical detach_subprocess) and ALSO killed the direct child only on all three termination paths, so it IS affected and was fixed the same way — it now imports reap_process_group and uses it on (a) the handshake-failure early return, (b) the terminal-emitted path (now sets released=true and falls through to the shared exit reap instead of a direct child.kill()), and (c) the final release/EOF/command-close exit block. Acquire-time stdin/stdout/stderr-unavailable error paths keep the direct child.kill() (child just spawned, no descendants forked yet). Regression test subprocess_release_reaps_whole_process_group (#[cfg(unix)]): mock adapter drives the subprocess path with `sh -c 'sh -c ": MARKER; sleep 3600" & printf up; sleep 3600'`, asserts the marker'd descendant is alive before release and gone after; a ProcessGroupGuard Drop-guard reaps defensively on any failure unwind, null stdio. MSRV-1.78-safe (tokio Child::try_wait/id/kill/wait, no post-1.78 std). Gates: cargo test -p orgasmic-drivers EXIT=0; cargo test -p orgasmic-daemon EXIT=0; cargo clippy --workspace --all-targets -D warnings EXIT=0; cargo fmt --check + git diff --check clean. Orphan proof: post-suite pgrep -fl "worker-server|sleep 3600|orgasmic-reap" -> none. Live smoke: ORGASMIC_LIVE_CURSOR_SMOKE=1 cargo test real_cursor_agent ran a real cursor-agent turn (1 passed, 9.13s) and post-run pgrep -fl "worker-server" -> none, proving the production release path reaps the real worker-server (the test guard is now a no-op belt-and-suspenders). Task flipped BACKLOG->IMPLEMENT->DONE.
:FROM_STATE:   backlog
:TO_STATE:     done
:END:

:MACHINE:      dev-machine.local
:PROJECT:      orgasmic
:TASK:         TASK-DMTDF.1
:TARGET:       crates/orgasmic-cli/tests/dispatch.rs
:REASON:       TASK-DMTDF.1 closed: added the end-to-end regression test the TASK-DMTDF reviewer flagged as missing (F-1 LOW) — committed tests asserted default-path distinctness via assert_ne! but never drove cmd_dispatch to the cross-kind worktree-collision bail. Verified the shipped semantics by reading crates/orgasmic-cli/src/manager.rs:286-303 (the cmd_dispatch path): after build_dispatch_plan, cmd_dispatch loops over [Implementer, Reviewer, Architector] and bails when other_kind != plan.kind && plan.worktree_path == default_worktree(first_task, other_kind), with error text "{} worktree must not reuse {} default path: {}" (DispatchKind Display == as_str()). The check fires BEFORE the --dry-run early return, so a dry-run dispatch exercises the bail with no worktree creation / no daemon dispatch / no worker spawn — no stub codex needed. New test dispatch_rejects_cross_kind_default_worktree_reuse (mirrors the existing run_orgasmic_failure + dry-run idiom; daemon booted then shut down per teardown discipline; PATH preserves system git via path_with_stub since build_dispatch_plan resolves --from/HEAD) exhausts the cross-kind matrix the loop guards: (1) --kind architector --worktree /tmp/orgasmic-worktrees/task-dispatch (implementer default) -> "architector worktree must not reuse implementer default path:"; (2) --kind architector --worktree /tmp/orgasmic-worktrees/task-dispatch-review (reviewer default) -> "architector worktree must not reuse reviewer default path:"; (3) --kind reviewer --worktree /tmp/orgasmic-worktrees/task-review-issues (implementer default) -> "reviewer worktree must not reuse implementer default path:". Uses BACKLOG TASK-DISPATCH (architector-dispatchable) + REVIEW TASK-REVIEW-ISSUES (reviewer-dispatchable) from seed_project; asserts none of the colliding paths were created on disk. Non-vacuity proven: replaced the guard with `if false && ...` -> test FAILED EXIT=101 (the architector dry-run succeeded and printed the plan, so run_orgasmic_failure panicked on unexpected success); restored to other_kind != plan.kind, production code unchanged in the commit.
